;;; MeTTa port of the Implication Direct Introduction PLN rule, using
;;; the match operator.
;;;
;;; (P a₁) ≞ p₁
;;; ...
;;; (P aₙ) ≞ pₙ
;;; (Q a₁) ≞ q₁
;;; ...
;;; (Q aₙ) ≞ qₙ
;;; ⊢
;;; P→Q ≞ tv
;;;
;;; where pᵢ (resp. qᵢ) are of boolean type representing whether (P aᵢ)
;;; (resp. (Q aᵢ)) has been observed as True or False, and tv
;;; represents the resulting truth value of the conclusion.
;; Import modules
!(import! &self "../common/OrderedSet.metta")

      -->(1,'&self',['import!','&self','../common/OrderedSet.metta'],depth(1))

%~   '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/interp_1/hyperon-pln_metta/match/ImplicationDirectIntroductionMatchTest.metta')

;; Definition of a set data structure.  Under the hood it is a sorted
;; list without duplicates, thus called OrderedSet.  For now its
;; constructor :: is unconstrained, meaning it does not guaranty that
;; the constructed OrderedSet are sorted and without duplicates.
;; Rather this is delegated to the insert function defined below.  In
;; order to guaranty that it is sorted without duplicates, the
;; constructor :: would need to take an additional argument encoding a
;; proof that the element to prepend is less than the head of the set
;; to be prepended to.
;;; Collection of functions operating on numbers
;; Define max
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,max,[->,A,A,A]])
  (: max 
    (-> $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[max,X,Y],[if,[>,X,Y],X,Y])
  (= 
    (max $X $Y) 
    (if 
      (> $X $Y) $X $Y))


;; Define min
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,min,[->,A,A,A]])
  (: min 
    (-> $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[min,X,Y],[if,[<,X,Y],X,Y])
  (= 
    (min $X $Y) 
    (if 
      (< $X $Y) $X $Y))


;; Clamp a number to be within a certain range
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,clamp,[->,A,A,A,A]])
  (: clamp 
    (-> $A $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[clamp,X,L,U],[max,L,[min,U,X]])
  (= 
    (clamp $X $L $U) 
    (max $L 
      (min $U $X)))


;; Define abs
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,abs,[->,A,A]])
  (: abs 
    (-> $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[abs,X],[if,[<,X,0],[*,-1,X],X])
  (= 
    (abs $X) 
    (if 
      (< $X 0) 
      (* -1 $X) $X))


;; Define <=
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,<=,[->,A,A,'Bool']])
  (: <= 
    (-> $A $A Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[<=,X,Y],[or,[<,X,Y],[==,X,Y]])
  (= 
    (<= $X $Y) 
    (or 
      (< $X $Y) 
      (== $X $Y)))


;; Define >=
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,>=,[->,A,A,'Bool']])
  (: >= 
    (-> $A $A Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[>=,X,Y],[or,[>,X,Y],[==,X,Y]])
  (= 
    (>= $X $Y) 
    (or 
      (> $X $Y) 
      (== $X $Y)))


;; Define approximately equal
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,approxEq,[->,A,A,A,'Bool']])
  (: approxEq 
    (-> $A $A $A Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[approxEq,X,Y,Epsilon],[<=,[abs,[-,X,Y]],Epsilon])
  (= 
    (approxEq $X $Y $Epsilon) 
    (<= 
      (abs 
        (- $X $Y)) $Epsilon))

;; TODO: alternatively we could have (: â¤ TruthValue) and (: â¥ TruthValue)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'Bl',[->,'Bool','TruthValue']])
  (: Bl 
    (-> Bool TruthValue))


;; First order probability TV constructor, i.e. mere probability.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'Pr',[->,'Number','TruthValue']])
  (: Pr 
    (-> Number TruthValue))


;; Simple Truth Value.  A Second order probability TV constructor,
;; i.e. probability and confidence.  The probability is in fact the
;; mode of the corresponding beta distribution.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'STV',[->,'Number','Number','TruthValue']])
  (: STV 
    (-> Number Number TruthValue))


;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Constants ;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; For now the underlying beta distributions have a Jeffreys prior,
;; i.e. the prior alpha and beta are 0.5.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'prior-alpha',[->,'Number']])
  (: prior-alpha 
    (-> Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['prior-alpha'],0.5)
  (= 
    (prior-alpha) 0.5)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'prior-beta',[->,'Number']])
  (: prior-beta 
    (-> Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['prior-beta'],0.5)
  (= 
    (prior-beta) 0.5)


;; Lookahead
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,lookahead,[->,'Number']])
  (: lookahead 
    (-> Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[lookahead],1.0)
  (= 
    (lookahead) 1.0)


;; Maximum supported count (till +inf is supported, possibly).
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'max-count',[->,'Number']])
  (: max-count 
    (-> Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['max-count'],1000000000.0)
  (= 
    (max-count) 1000000000.0)


;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Methods ;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Convert count to confidence using the formula
;;
;; confidence = count / (count + lookahead)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'count->confidence',[->,'Number','Number']])
  (: count->confidence 
    (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['count->confidence',Cnt],[/,Cnt,[+,Cnt,[lookahead]]])
  (= 
    (count->confidence $Cnt) 
    (/ $Cnt 
      (+ $Cnt 
        (lookahead))))


;; Convert confidence to count using the formula
;;
;; count = (confidence * lookahead) / (1 - confidence)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'confidence->count',[->,'Number','Number']])
  (: confidence->count 
    (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['confidence->count',Conf],[if,[approxEq,1.0,Conf,1.0e-9],['max-count'],[/,[*,Conf,[lookahead]],[-,1.0,Conf]]])
  (= 
    (confidence->count $Conf) 
    (if 
      (approxEq 1.0 $Conf 1.0e-9) 
      (max-count) 
      (/ 
        (* $Conf 
          (lookahead)) 
        (- 1.0 $Conf))))


;; Increment the negative count of a given truth value, by
;; incrementing its total count without incrementing the positive
;; count.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'inc-neg-count',[->,'TruthValue','TruthValue']])
  (: inc-neg-count 
    (-> TruthValue TruthValue))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['inc-neg-count',['STV',S,C]],['let*',[[Tot_cnt,['confidence->count',C]],[Pos_cnt,[*,S,Tot_cnt]],[New_tot_cnt,[+,Tot_cnt,1]]],['STV',[/,Pos_cnt,New_tot_cnt],['count->confidence',New_tot_cnt]]])
  (= 
    (inc-neg-count 
      (STV $S $C)) 
    (let* 
      ( ($Tot_cnt 
          (confidence->count $C)) 
        ($Pos_cnt 
          (* $S $Tot_cnt)) 
        ($New_tot_cnt 
          (+ $Tot_cnt 1))) 
      (STV 
        (/ $Pos_cnt $New_tot_cnt) 
        (count->confidence $New_tot_cnt))))


;; Increment the positive count of a given truth value, by
;; incrementing its total count and its positive count.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'inc-pos-count',[->,'TruthValue','TruthValue']])
  (: inc-pos-count 
    (-> TruthValue TruthValue))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['inc-pos-count',['STV',S,C]],['let*',[[Tot_cnt,['confidence->count',C]],[Pos_cnt,[*,S,Tot_cnt]],[New_pos_cnt,[+,Pos_cnt,1]],[New_tot_cnt,[+,Tot_cnt,1]]],['STV',[/,New_pos_cnt,New_tot_cnt],['count->confidence',New_tot_cnt]]])
  (= 
    (inc-pos-count 
      (STV $S $C)) 
    (let* 
      ( ($Tot_cnt 
          (confidence->count $C)) 
        ($Pos_cnt 
          (* $S $Tot_cnt)) 
        ($New_pos_cnt 
          (+ $Pos_cnt 1)) 
        ($New_tot_cnt 
          (+ $Tot_cnt 1))) 
      (STV 
        (/ $New_pos_cnt $New_tot_cnt) 
        (count->confidence $New_tot_cnt))))


;; Return the first order probability mode of the second order
;; distribution associated to a truth value.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,mode,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: mode 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['Bl','True']],1.0)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (Bl True)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['Bl','False']],0.0)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (Bl False)) 0.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['Pr',Pr]],Pr)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (Pr $Pr)) $Pr)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['STV',Pr,_]],Pr)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (STV $Pr $_)) $Pr)


;; Return the total count of a truth value.  For truth values not
;; capturing a notion of confidence, such as Bl or Pr then the count
;; is assumed to be a very large number (cause +inf does not seem to
;; be supported at the moment).
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,count,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: count 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[count,['Bl',_]],['max-count'])
  (= 
    (count 
      (Bl $_)) 
    (max-count))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[count,['Pr',_]],['max-count'])
  (= 
    (count 
      (Pr $_)) 
    (max-count))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[count,['STV',_,Conf]],['confidence->count',Conf])
  (= 
    (count 
      (STV $_ $Conf)) 
    (confidence->count $Conf))


;; Return the confidence of a truth value.  For truth values not
;; capturing a notion of confidence, such as Bl or Pr then the
;; confidence is assumed to be 1.0.  For truth values capturing a
;; notion of confidence, such as STV, the formula to convert a count
;; into confidence is as follows
;;
;; confidence = count / (count + lookahead)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,confidence,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: confidence 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[confidence,['Bl',_]],1.0)
  (= 
    (confidence 
      (Bl $_)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[confidence,['Pr',_]],1.0)
  (= 
    (confidence 
      (Pr $_)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[confidence,['STV',_,Conf]],Conf)
  (= 
    (confidence 
      (STV $_ $Conf)) $Conf)


;; Return the positive count of a truth value.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'pos-count',[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: pos-count 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['pos-count',Tv],[*,[mode,Tv],[count,Tv]])
  (= 
    (pos-count $Tv) 
    (* 
      (mode $Tv) 
      (count $Tv)))


;; Return the negative count of a truth value.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'neg-count',[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: neg-count 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['neg-count',Tv],[*,[-,1,[mode,Tv]],[count,Tv]])
  (= 
    (neg-count $Tv) 
    (* 
      (- 1 
        (mode $Tv)) 
      (count $Tv)))


;; Return the posterior alpha of a truth value
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'post-alpha',[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: post-alpha 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['post-alpha',Tv],[+,['prior-alpha'],['pos-count',Tv]])
  (= 
    (post-alpha $Tv) 
    (+ 
      (prior-alpha) 
      (pos-count $Tv)))


;; Return the posterior beta of a truth value
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'post-beta',[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: post-beta 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['post-beta',Tv],[+,['prior-beta'],['neg-count',Tv]])
  (= 
    (post-beta $Tv) 
    (+ 
      (prior-beta) 
      (neg-count $Tv)))


;; Return the first order probability mean of the second order
;; distribution associated to a truth value.  For truth values not
;; capturing a notion of confidence, such as Bl or Pr then the
;; confidence is assumed to be 1.0.  For truth values capturing a
;; notion of confidence, such as STV, a beta distribution is assumed.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,mean,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: mean 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mean,['Bl','True']],1.0)
  (= 
    (mean 
      (Bl True)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mean,['Bl','False']],0.0)
  (= 
    (mean 
      (Bl False)) 0.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mean,['Pr',Pr]],Pr)
  (= 
    (mean 
      (Pr $Pr)) $Pr)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mean,['STV',Pr,Conf]],['let*',[[A,['post-alpha',['STV',Pr,Conf]]],[B,['post-beta',['STV',Pr,Conf]]]],[/,A,[+,A,B]]])
  (= 
    (mean 
      (STV $Pr $Conf)) 
    (let* 
      ( ($A 
          (post-alpha 
            (STV $Pr $Conf))) 
        ($B 
          (post-beta 
            (STV $Pr $Conf)))) 
      (/ $A 
        (+ $A $B))))


      <--(4,retval('Empty'))

  (: pos_count 
    (-> EvidentialTruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[pos_count,['ETV',Ev,Tv]],[*,[mode,Tv],[count,Tv]])
  (= 
    (pos_count 
      (ETV $Ev $Tv)) 
    (* 
      (mode $Tv) 
      (count $Tv)))


;; Return the negative count of a truth value.

      (ETV $Ev $Tv))

      (- 1 
        (mode $Tv)) 
      (count $Tv)))

  (: post_alpha

  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[post_alpha,['ETV',Ev,Tv]],[+,[prior_alpha],[pos_count,Tv]])

      (prior_alpha)

  (=

      (ETV $Ev $Tv))

      (prior_beta) 
      (neg_count $Tv)))

  (=

      (> $X $Y) $X $Y))

    (clamp $X $L $U) 
    (max $L 
      (min $U $X)))

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'TruthValue','Type'])
  (: TruthValue Type)


;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Constructors ;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Boolean TV constructor
;; TODO: alternatively we could have (: â¤ TruthValue) and (: â¥ TruthValue)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'Bl',[->,'Bool','TruthValue']])
  (: Bl 
    (-> Bool TruthValue))


;; First order probability TV constructor, i.e. mere probability.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'Pr',[->,'Number','TruthValue']])
  (: Pr 
    (-> Number TruthValue))


;; Simple Truth Value.  A Second order probability TV constructor,
;; i.e. probability and confidence.  The probability is in fact the
;; mode of the corresponding beta distribution.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'STV',[->,'Number','Number','TruthValue']])
  (: STV 
    (-> Number Number TruthValue))


;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Constants ;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; For now the underlying beta distributions have a Jeffreys prior,
;; i.e. the prior alpha and beta are 0.5.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'prior-alpha',[->,'Number']])
  (: prior-alpha 
    (-> Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['prior-alpha'],0.5)
  (= 
    (prior-alpha) 0.5)


  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'prior-beta',[->,'Number']])
  (: prior-beta 
    (-> Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['prior-beta'],0.5)
  (= 
    (prior-beta) 0.5)


;; Lookahead
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,lookahead,[->,'Number']])
  (: lookahead 
    (-> Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[lookahead],1.0)
  (= 
    (lookahead) 1.0)


;; Maximum supported count (till +inf is supported, possibly).
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'max-count',[->,'Number']])
  (: max-count 
    (-> Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['max-count'],1000000000.0)
  (= 
    (max-count) 1000000000.0)


;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Methods ;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;; Convert count to confidence using the formula
;;
;; confidence = count / (count + lookahead)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'count->confidence',[->,'Number','Number']])
  (: count->confidence 
    (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['count->confidence',Cnt],[/,Cnt,[+,Cnt,[lookahead]]])
  (= 
    (count->confidence $Cnt) 
    (/ $Cnt 
      (+ $Cnt 
        (lookahead))))


;; Convert confidence to count using the formula
;;
;; count = (confidence * lookahead) / (1 - confidence)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'confidence->count',[->,'Number','Number']])
  (: confidence->count 
    (-> Number Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['confidence->count',Conf],[if,[approxEq,1.0,Conf,1.0e-9],['max-count'],[/,[*,Conf,[lookahead]],[-,1.0,Conf]]])
  (= 
    (confidence->count $Conf) 
    (if 
      (approxEq 1.0 $Conf 1.0e-9) 
      (max-count) 
      (/ 
        (* $Conf 
          (lookahead)) 
        (- 1.0 $Conf))))


;; Increment the negative count of a given truth value, by
;; incrementing its total count without incrementing the positive
;; count.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'inc-neg-count',[->,'TruthValue','TruthValue']])
  (: inc-neg-count 
    (-> TruthValue TruthValue))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['inc-neg-count',['STV',S,C]],['let*',[[Tot_cnt,['confidence->count',C]],[Pos_cnt,[*,S,Tot_cnt]],[New_tot_cnt,[+,Tot_cnt,1]]],['STV',[/,Pos_cnt,New_tot_cnt],['count->confidence',New_tot_cnt]]])
  (= 
    (inc-neg-count 
      (STV $S $C)) 
    (let* 
      ( ($Tot_cnt 
          (confidence->count $C)) 
        ($Pos_cnt 
          (* $S $Tot_cnt)) 
        ($New_tot_cnt 
          (+ $Tot_cnt 1))) 
      (STV 
        (/ $Pos_cnt $New_tot_cnt) 
        (count->confidence $New_tot_cnt))))


;; Increment the positive count of a given truth value, by
;; incrementing its total count and its positive count.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'inc-pos-count',[->,'TruthValue','TruthValue']])
  (: inc-pos-count 
    (-> TruthValue TruthValue))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['inc-pos-count',['STV',S,C]],['let*',[[Tot_cnt,['confidence->count',C]],[Pos_cnt,[*,S,Tot_cnt]],[New_pos_cnt,[+,Pos_cnt,1]],[New_tot_cnt,[+,Tot_cnt,1]]],['STV',[/,New_pos_cnt,New_tot_cnt],['count->confidence',New_tot_cnt]]])
  (= 
    (inc-pos-count 
      (STV $S $C)) 
    (let* 
      ( ($Tot_cnt 
          (confidence->count $C)) 
        ($Pos_cnt 
          (* $S $Tot_cnt)) 
        ($New_pos_cnt 
          (+ $Pos_cnt 1)) 
        ($New_tot_cnt 
          (+ $Tot_cnt 1))) 
      (STV 
        (/ $New_pos_cnt $New_tot_cnt) 
        (count->confidence $New_tot_cnt))))


;; Return the first order probability mode of the second order
;; distribution associated to a truth value.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,mode,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: mode 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['Bl','True']],1.0)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (Bl True)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['Bl','False']],0.0)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (Bl False)) 0.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['Pr',Pr]],Pr)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (Pr $Pr)) $Pr)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mode,['STV',Pr,_]],Pr)
  (= 
    (mode 
      (STV $Pr $_)) $Pr)


;; Return the total count of a truth value.  For truth values not
;; capturing a notion of confidence, such as Bl or Pr then the count
;; is assumed to be a very large number (cause +inf does not seem to
;; be supported at the moment).
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,count,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: count 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[count,['Bl',_]],['max-count'])
  (= 
    (count 
      (Bl $_)) 
    (max-count))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[count,['Pr',_]],['max-count'])
  (= 
    (count 
      (Pr $_)) 
    (max-count))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[count,['STV',_,Conf]],['confidence->count',Conf])
  (= 
    (count 
      (STV $_ $Conf)) 
    (confidence->count $Conf))


;; Return the confidence of a truth value.  For truth values not
;; capturing a notion of confidence, such as Bl or Pr then the
;; confidence is assumed to be 1.0.  For truth values capturing a
;; notion of confidence, such as STV, the formula to convert a count
;; into confidence is as follows
;;
;; confidence = count / (count + lookahead)
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,confidence,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: confidence 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[confidence,['Bl',_]],1.0)
  (= 
    (confidence 
      (Bl $_)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[confidence,['Pr',_]],1.0)
  (= 
    (confidence 
      (Pr $_)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[confidence,['STV',_,Conf]],Conf)
  (= 
    (confidence 
      (STV $_ $Conf)) $Conf)


;; Return the positive count of a truth value.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'pos-count',[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: pos-count 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['pos-count',Tv],[*,[mode,Tv],[count,Tv]])
  (= 
    (pos-count $Tv) 
    (* 
      (mode $Tv) 
      (count $Tv)))


;; Return the negative count of a truth value.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'neg-count',[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: neg-count 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['neg-count',Tv],[*,[-,1,[mode,Tv]],[count,Tv]])
  (= 
    (neg-count $Tv) 
    (* 
      (- 1 
        (mode $Tv)) 
      (count $Tv)))


;; Return the posterior alpha of a truth value
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'post-alpha',[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: post-alpha 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['post-alpha',Tv],[+,['prior-alpha'],['pos-count',Tv]])
  (= 
    (post-alpha $Tv) 
    (+ 
      (prior-alpha) 
      (pos-count $Tv)))


;; Return the posterior beta of a truth value
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'post-beta',[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: post-beta 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['post-beta',Tv],[+,['prior-beta'],['neg-count',Tv]])
  (= 
    (post-beta $Tv) 
    (+ 
      (prior-beta) 
      (neg-count $Tv)))


;; Return the first order probability mean of the second order
;; distribution associated to a truth value.  For truth values not
;; capturing a notion of confidence, such as Bl or Pr then the
;; confidence is assumed to be 1.0.  For truth values capturing a
;; notion of confidence, such as STV, a beta distribution is assumed.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,mean,[->,'TruthValue','Number']])
  (: mean 
    (-> TruthValue Number))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mean,['Bl','True']],1.0)
  (= 
    (mean 
      (Bl True)) 1.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mean,['Bl','False']],0.0)
  (= 
    (mean 
      (Bl False)) 0.0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mean,['Pr',Pr]],Pr)
  (= 
    (mean 
      (Pr $Pr)) $Pr)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[mean,['STV',Pr,Conf]],['let*',[[A,['post-alpha',['STV',Pr,Conf]]],[B,['post-beta',['STV',Pr,Conf]]]],[/,A,[+,A,B]]])
  (= 
    (mean 
      (STV $Pr $Conf)) 
    (let* 
      ( ($A 
          (post-alpha 
            (STV $Pr $Conf))) 
        ($B 
          (post-beta 
            (STV $Pr $Conf)))) 
      (/ $A 
        (+ $A $B))))

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'direct-introduction-base-formula',[->,'Bool','TruthValue']])

;; Alternate implication direct introduction formula.  Inductive case,

;; Recursive step (inductive rule):
;;
;; (p a) â patv
;; (q a) â qatv
;; pâq â (ETV ev pqtv)
;; a â ev
;; â¢
;; pâq â (ETV (insert a ev) tv)
;;
;; where tv is calculated as defined in the idi_formula.
;;
;; IDI rule as a function
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[idi_induction,['â\x89\\x9E\',[P,A],Patv],['â\x89\\x9E\',[Q,A],Qatv],['â\x89\\x9E\',['â\x86\\x92\',P,Q],['ETV',Ev,Pqtv]],['â\x88\\x89\',A,Ev]],['â\x89\\x9E\',['â\x86\\x92\',P,Q],['ETV',[insert,A,Ev],[idi_formula,Patv,Qatv,Pqtv]]])

    (idi_induction 
      (â 
        ($P $A) $Patv) 
      (â 
        ($Q $A) $Qatv) 
      (â 
        (â $P $Q) 
        (ETV $Ev $Pqtv)) 
      (â $A $Ev)) 
    (â 
      (â $P $Q) 
      (ETV 
        (insert $A $Ev) 
        (idi_formula $Patv $Qatv $Pqtv))))


; Corresponding matching query of IDI rule
;;; There is a bug with MeTTa interpreter in using let* for this matching query,
; as it matches ($p $a), ($q $a) with (= (idi_induction_match $kb) ...) pattern.

; to set Type (: â (-> Atom Atom Atom)), but using such Type causes the evaluations
; inside the conclusion to don't get reduced. So, I am not using let* until gets fixed.
